NID 6 is 'Sansation-BoldItalic', Everything looks good.

Mac NID 6

NID 6 is 'Sansation-Light', Everything looks good.

Sansation Light Light Italic (Sansation-LightItalic.ttf)

name

Mac NID 6

Mac NID 6, PostScript Name check for illegal characters.
Monotype uses NID 6 for creating CSS classes for their demo HTML. The following characters cause issues in the CSS code: '
, , , &, _, [, ], (, ), {, }, <, >, /, \, %'

NID 6 is 'Sansation-LightItalic', Everything looks good.

Pass

Kerning (kern Table and GPOS Kerning)

Kerning (kern Table and GPOS Kerning)

Error

Sansation Regular (Sansation-Regular.ttf)

GPOS

kern

Simple check if kern feature in GPOS table.

GPOS table does not have kerning feature. Please investigate if this meets requirements.

Warning

Sansation Regular (Sansation-Regular.ttf)

kern

-/-

Check if 'kern' table in TTF font.

Font has 'kern' table. Please verify if font requires kern table or if only GPOS kerning should be in font.
For example: PowerPoint only supports a flat GPOS kerning or a kern table. So, if the customer requires PowerPoint support, a kern table is necessary.

Error

OS/2 and head

sTypeAsc/Desc and unitsPerEm

The result of sTypoAscender – sTypoDescender should match or exceed the unitsPerEm value.

The result of sTypoAscender – sTypoDescender (2292) match or exceed the unitsPerEm value (2048).
